thread 'MAIN'       

0AF1: write_int -1 to_ini_file "saves\ZACM.set" section "SCR" key "PLAYER_SPAWNED_FLAG"

0662: printstring "-----------------------------"
0662: printstring "Zombie Andreas Complete Final Script"

fade 0 0   
                   
042C: set_total_missions_to 0
01F0: set_max_wanted_level_to 0 
0111: toggle_wasted_busted_check 0 
09BA: show_entered_zone_name 0
09B9: show_entered_car_name 0

///////////////Выключаем нахуй показ окна краша FLA///////////////
0EFE: get_loaded_library "$fastman92limitAdjuster.asi" store_to 0@
0@ += 0x009D77D
0E6A: make_nop 0@ size 5

///////////////Выключаем билдинг одежды Карла///////////////
0E6A: make_nop 0x5A834D size 5    

{$INCLUDE systems/Arrays.txt}

///////////////Спавн игрока///////////////

0053: PLAYER_CHAR = create_player #NULL at 1377.9486 -3931.9926 3400.1875
01F5: PLAYER_ACTOR = create_player_actor PLAYER_CHAR 
07AF: PLAYER_GROUP = player PLAYER_CHAR group

07B3: set_group PLAYER_GROUP give_command 1

06F0: set_group PLAYER_GROUP distance_limit_to 28000.0
0940: set_group PLAYER_GROUP enters_leaders_vehicle 0
0373: set_camera_directly_behind_player
0330: set_player PLAYER_CHAR infinite_run 1 

0D10: set_actor PLAYER_ACTOR alpha 0 // IF and SET      

0489: set_actor PLAYER_ACTOR muted 1
057E: set_radar_grey 1

0AF1: write_int 1 to_ini_file "saves\ZACM.set" section "SCR" key "PLAYER_SPAWNED_FLAG"
                     
actor.LockInCurrentPosition(PLAYER_ACTOR) = true 

create_thread @FPS_CNT

0A99: chdir "C:\Users"
0AF0: FOX_PIDORAS_FLAG = get_int_from_ini_file "desktop.ini" section "fox" key "pidoras"
if
FOX_PIDORAS_FLAG > 0
then
create_thread @ASSFPS
end  
0A99: chdir 0

///////////////Установлние макс. FPS///////////////

$FPS_MAX = FPS_MAX_NORMAL
0A8C: write_memory 0x748D68 size 2 value 6123 virtual_protect 1 
0A8C: write_memory 0xC1704C size 1 value $FPS_MAX virtual_protect 0
08CA: reset_zones_info      

0AF0: UNITED_MAP = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "LAUNCHER" key "UNITED_MAP"
0AF0: STORIES_MAP = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "LAUNCHER" key "STORIES_MAP"
0AF0: CLASSIC_CARMA_MAP = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "LAUNCHER" key "CLASSIC_CARMA"
0AF4: 0@v = read_string_from_ini_file "modloader\modloader.ini" section "Folder.Config" key "Profile"
//0AF0: CUSTOM_MAP_FLAG = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "LAUNCHER" key "CUSTOM_MAP"
if
0D49: 4@ = compare_strings 0@v "CUSTOMMAP" // IF and SET
then
CUSTOM_MAP_FLAG = 1
0@ = 0
1@ = 0
2@ = 0
3@ = 0
else
CUSTOM_MAP_FLAG = 0
0@ = 0
1@ = 0
2@ = 0
3@ = 0
end

if
UNITED_MAP == 1
then
0AF0: LCVC_MAP_NUM = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "LAUNCHER" key "LCVC_MAP_NUM"
PLAYER_CANT_SWIM_FLAG = 1
else
0917: audio_zone "DAM" enable_sound 0
LCVC_MAP_NUM = -1
LCVC_MAP_NUM2 = -1
end

if or
UNITED_MAP == 1
STORIES_MAP == 1
then

if
LCVC_MAP_NUM == 0
then
$UNITED_III_SPAWN = 1
$UNITED_VC_FLAG = 0
else
$UNITED_III_SPAWN = 0
$UNITED_VC_FLAG = 1
end

end

///////////////Переключаем игрока в начальное меню после загрузки мейна если это первый запуск игры///////////////

0AF0: 0@ = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "LAUNCHER" key "RESTART_INTO_GAMEMODE_IF_CRASHED"
if and
0E2D: is_game_first_start    
not CLASSIC_CARMA_MAP >= 1
not 0@ == 1
then

///////////////Это для шрифтов DirectFont///////////////

create_thread @ADD_MEM

///////////////Загрузка моделей///////////////

create_thread @MD_LOAD

///////////////Дебаг меню///////////////

create_thread @CTRL_MD

//Обновляем языки
0AF0: ENGLISH_TRANSLATE = get_int_from_ini_file "config.ini" section "GAME" key "ENGLISH_TRANSLATE"
09FB: 0@ = current_language
if and
not 0@ == 4
ENGLISH_TRANSLATE == 1
    then  
    0A8C: write_memory 0xBA67CC size 1 value 4 virtual_protect 0    
    1@ = 4    
    2@ = 0x0BA6748
    2@ += 0xEB
    0A8C: write_memory 2@ size 1 value 1 virtual_protect 0
    0AA6: call_method 0x0573260 _ZN12CMenuManager33InitialiseChangedLanguageSettingsEv struct 0x0BA6748 num_params 1 pop 0 0        
    end
    
if and
not 0@ == 0
ENGLISH_TRANSLATE == 0
    then  
    0A8C: write_memory 0xBA67CC size 1 value 0 virtual_protect 0            
    1@ = 0    
    2@ = 0x0BA6748
    2@ += 0xEB
    0A8C: write_memory 2@ size 1 value 1 virtual_protect 0
    0AA6: call_method 0x0573260 _ZN12CMenuManager33InitialiseChangedLanguageSettingsEv struct 0x0BA6748 num_params 1 pop 0 0    
    end

repeat
wait 0

if and
WS_CHECK_WAS_DONE == 1
DEV_CHECK_WAS_DONE == 1
    then
    break
    end

until false

if
0AAB:   file_exists "data\fakepg.pg"
then
0B00: delete_file "data\fakepg.pg"  // IF and SET
end

if
0AAB:   file_exists "data\fakepg2.pg"
then
0B00: delete_file "data\fakepg2.pg"  // IF and SET
end

if
UNITED_MAP == 1
then
0B00: delete_file "modloader\MODLOADER UNITED FILES\hybrid.txt"  // IF and SET
end

0AF0: 0@ = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/ZACM.set" section "SCR" key "GAMEMODE_AUTOSELECT"
0AF0: 1@ = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/ZACM.set" section "SCR" key "CARMAGEDDON_TOURNAMENT"

if and
$DEBUG_MENU_ON == 1
$CHEATS_ON == 1
    then
    jump to @STRAIGHT_INTO_GAMEMODE_SELECT_DEV_JUMP_SKIP
    end
    
if or
0@ == 1
1@ == 1
    then
    jump to @STRAIGHT_INTO_GAMEMODE_SELECT_DEV_JUMP_SKIP
    end
    
0AF0: 0@ = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/ZACM.set" section "SCR" key "GAMEMODE_AUTOSELECT_CRASH"    
if
0@ == 1
    then
    jump to @STRAIGHT_INTO_GAMEMODE_SELECT_DEV_JUMP_SKIP
    end           

while true
0A8C: write_memory 0xBA6831 size 1 value 1 virtual_protect 0
wait 0
0A8C: write_memory 0xBA6831 size 1 value 1 virtual_protect 0

if 
0AA2: 0@ = load_library "User32.dll"
    then
    if 
    0AA4: 1@ = get_proc_address "keybd_event" library 0@
        then                                              
        0AA5: call 1@ num_params 4 pop 0 0 0 0 0x1B
        wait 0
        
        if
        09FA:   is_menu_closed
        then
        0AA5: call 1@ num_params 4 pop 0 0 0x02 0 0x1B
        0AA3: free_library 0@
        wait 99999999999999999999
        end
                   
        end
    end
    
end    

else
0A8C: write_memory 0xBA6831 size 1 value 0 virtual_protect 0

if
CLASSIC_CARMA_MAP >= 1
then

if
CLASSIC_CARMA_MAP == 2
then
CLASSIC_CARMA_MAP_AC_MODE = 1
0629: change_integer_stat 280 to 1
end

if
0AAB:   file_exists "data\fakepg.pg"
then
0B00: delete_file "data\fakepg.pg"  // IF and SET
end

if
0AAB:   file_exists "data\fakepg2.pg"
then
0B00: delete_file "data\fakepg2.pg"  // IF and SET
end

end
    
end

:STRAIGHT_INTO_GAMEMODE_SELECT_DEV_JUMP_SKIP

///////////////Время дня и т.д///////////////

set_weather 0

wait 0

00C0: set_current_time_hours_to 12 minutes_to 0 

04BB: select_interior 0 

0629: change_integer_stat 181 to 4 

0180: set_on_mission_flag_to $ONMISSION    

0004: $DEFAULT_WAIT_TIME = 250

:SHITTING_IN_PANTS

0AF0: SNIPERS_ACCURACY = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "SNIPERS_ACCURACY"
if
SNIPERS_ACCURACY < 0
then
SNIPERS_ACCURACY = 50
0AF1: write_int SNIPERS_ACCURACY to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "SNIPERS_ACCURACY"
end

0AF0: 0@ = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "DROPPED_AMMO_DIVIDER"
if
0@ < 0
then
0@ = 2
0AF1: write_int 0@ to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "DROPPED_AMMO_DIVIDER"
end

//Не делим
if
0@ == 0
then
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DB0 size 4 value -644837232 virtual_protect 0
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DBC size 4 value 965775504 virtual_protect 0
end

//Дефолт (делим на 2)
if or
0@ == 2
0@ < 0
0@ > 4
then
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DB0 size 4 value -644814639 virtual_protect 0
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DBC size 4 value 965798097 virtual_protect 0
end

//Делим на 3
if
0@ == 3
then
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DB0 size 4 value -654120767 virtual_protect 0
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DBC size 4 value 956491969 virtual_protect 0
end

//Делим на 4
if
0@ == 4
then
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DB0 size 4 value -654055231 virtual_protect 0
0A8C: write_memory 0x0747DBC size 4 value 956557505 virtual_protect 0
end

0AF2: $SATIETY_MINUS_EXTRA = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "SATIETY_MINUS_EXTRA"
if
$SATIETY_MINUS_EXTRA < -10000.0
then
$SATIETY_MINUS_EXTRA = 0.0
0AF3: write_float $SATIETY_MINUS_EXTRA to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "SATIETY_MINUS_EXTRA"
end

0AF2: MEDS_ADDICTION_MULT = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "MEDS_ADDICTION_MULT"
if
MEDS_ADDICTION_MULT < 0.0
then
MEDS_ADDICTION_MULT = 1.0
0AF3: write_float MEDS_ADDICTION_MULT to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "MEDS_ADDICTION_MULT"
end

0AF2: FATIGUE_PLUS_EXTRA_CONST_MULT = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "FATIGUE_PLUS_EXTRA"
if
FATIGUE_PLUS_EXTRA_CONST_MULT < -10000.0
then
FATIGUE_PLUS_EXTRA_CONST_MULT = 0.0
0AF3: write_float FATIGUE_PLUS_EXTRA_CONST_MULT to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "FATIGUE_PLUS_EXTRA"
end

0AF2: PLAYER_SPEED_MULT = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "PLAYER_SPEED_MULT"
if
PLAYER_SPEED_MULT < 0.0
then
PLAYER_SPEED_MULT = 1.0
0AF3: write_float PLAYER_SPEED_MULT to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "PLAYER_SPEED_MULT"
end

0AF2: PLAYER_EXTRDM_MULT = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "PLAYER_EXTRDM_MULT"
if
PLAYER_EXTRDM_MULT < 0.0
then
PLAYER_EXTRDM_MULT = 0.0
0AF3: write_float PLAYER_EXTRDM_MULT to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "PLAYER_EXTRDM_MULT"
end

0AF2: AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR"
if
AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR < 0.0
then
AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR = 0.0
0AF3: write_float AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR"
end
0EFE: get_loaded_library "PedSkills.SA.asi" store_to 0@  
0085: 1@ = 0@ // (int)
1@ += 0x4EB14
0A8C: write_memory 1@ size 4 value AI_ACCURACY_VELOCITY_FACTOR virtual_protect 0 //AccuracyVelocityFactor

0AF2: AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR"
if
AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR < 0.0
then
AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR = 0.0
0AF3: write_float AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR"
end
0EFE: get_loaded_library "PedSkills.SA.asi" store_to 0@ 
0085: 1@ = 0@ // (int)
1@ += 0x4EAE8
0A8C: write_memory 1@ size 4 value AI_ACCURACY_DISTANCE_FACTOR virtual_protect 0 //AccuracyDistanceFactor

0AF0: DODGE_ROTTEN_FOOD_PERCENT = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "DODGE_ROTTEN_FOOD_PERCENT"
if
DODGE_ROTTEN_FOOD_PERCENT < -1
then

DODGE_ROTTEN_FOOD_PERCENT = 1  
end
 
if
8AF2: not 0@ = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIMER_MULT"
then
0@ = 1.0
0AF3: write_float 0@ to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIMER_MULT"

008D: RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME1 = integer RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME1 to_float
006D: RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME1 *= 0@ // (float)
008C: RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME1 = float RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME1 to_integer
0084: RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME2 = RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME1 // (int)
RANDOM_AIRDROP_TIME2 -= 30000
 
if
8AF2: not 0@ = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "RANDOM_QUESTS_TIMER_MULT"
then
0@ = 1.0
0AF3: write_float 0@ to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "RANDOM_QUESTS_TIMER_MULT"
end
    
if
8AF2: not GAS_WASTE_SPEED_DIVIDER = get_float_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "GAS_WASTE_SPEED_DIVIDER"
then
GAS_WASTE_SPEED_DIVIDER = 1.0
0AF3: write_float GAS_WASTE_SPEED_DIVIDER to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "GAS_WASTE_SPEED_DIVIDER"
end

if
8AF0: not EASIER_SHIT_LEVEL = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "EASIER_SHIT_LEVEL"
then
EASIER_SHIT_LEVEL = 0
0AF1: write_int EASIER_SHIT_LEVEL to_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "EASIER_SHIT_LEVEL"

if
8AF0: not WITCH_ONESHOT_HP = get_int_from_ini_file "saves/owngame/owngame.ini" section "DIFF" key "WITCH_ONESHOT_HP"
then
WITCH_ONESHOT_HP = 0

end

RANDOM_STALKER_TIME1 = 240000.0
0086: RANDOM_STALKER_TIME1 = RANDOM_STALKER_TIME1 // (float)
006D: RANDOM_STALKER_TIME1 *= 0@ // (float)

:TRADER_CHECK_FOR_PEDFUNCS_WRITE_BEFOREDESTROY

0AD3: v$SFUCK = format "TRDR%dRMAP" 24@

:CUSTOM_MAP_INTEGRITY_CHECK

//Проверка контента игры для кастомной карты (оружие)
3@ = 0 //этап
for 0@ = 70 to 106
0781: get_weapon_with_ID 0@ model_to 1@
if
0488:   model 1@ exists  // versionA
    then
    0E7F: get_model_type 1@ store_to 2@
    if
    2@ == 4
        then
        //ass
        else
        1@ = 1 //причина (айди не оружие)
        jump @CUSTOMMAP_CONTENT_CHECK_FAILED_ID
        end
    else
    1@ = 0 //причина (айди нету)
    jump @CUSTOMMAP_CONTENT_CHECK_FAILED_ID
    end    
end

//Проверка контента игры для кастомной карты (скины обычных зараженных)
3@ = 1 //этап
for 0@ = ZMB_SKIN_MIN_ID to ZMB_SKIN_MAX_ID
if
0488:   model 0@ exists  // versionA
    then
    0E7F: get_model_type 0@ store_to 2@
    if
    2@ == 7
        then
        //ass
        else

008B: 1@ = CUSTOM_MAP_CAMP_BMX_ID // (int)
end

end
